New Early Rice Arrives in Market, Price Drops by Half a Yuan 123

South Market: Yesterday, sources numbered 20-30. Urban and rural shops were selling. The weather was clear and sunny, but buying interest seemed low and trading appetite was weak. As a result, prices were slightly soft. Thick japonica rice saw a small decline of 0.2 yuan. Thin indica rice arrivals were slightly more receptive, but supply of Ningbo rice remained scarce. Street sales were moving, but sporadically, and prices were also down 0.1-0.2 yuan. Reed-ocean premium goods were sparsely sold but remained firm in shape. Silver dollars for cash sales were flat, with no gains or losses. New early rice from Pudong arrived yesterday, with over forty stones. The opening price was slightly less than half a yuan. Shenli, Xinchang, Yuchengtai, and Hecheng four companies purchased it. Imported rice was also seeing thinner customer demand due to the clear and sunny weather, and the street market was particularly quiet. The market showed a weak and sluggish state.

New Rice Market: Yesterday, the weather cleared up. There were very few people at the early morning market. Thick japonica rice, high and secondary grades, fell back by 0.2-0.3 yuan. Arrivals of thin indica rice surged, but sales were sluggish. Inventory remained high, and the situation led to a drop of 0.4-0.5 yuan. Reed-ocean premium rice saw poor customer demand, but prices did not rise or fall. Glutinous rice river inventory was scarce, with only three bamboo tubes remaining. After a few pecks were sold, the overall price increased by nearly a foot. The second batch of new early rice from Zhoupu, around 100 dan, arrived, and various rice mills were selling it. Market conditions were similar to those in the southern district. Boats arriving from inner roads were numbered 21-22.

Flour Buying Interest Revives 124

Distant Futures Improve by One Cent

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, prices for various months initially showed a flat and then rising trend. Because the price of imported wheat only improved by about 0.1-0.2 yuan, most factories were wary due to the large batches released at the end of the previous week. Later, due to the ongoing flood disasters in various places, with the Gaoyou dam bursting and the water volume in the Yangtze River area increasing rather than decreasing, buying interest revived, and absorption occurred step by step. Factories remained calm and cautious, with very few batches released. Observation suggests that the situation may temporarily stabilize, as the courage of the inland groups has not yet declined. As a result, the price for this month remained unchanged compared to the end of the previous week, September improved by 0.05 percent, October improved by 0.1 percent, November/December improved by 0.125 percent, and January improved by 0.175 percent.

Wheat Market Sees Another Surge 125

13,000 Bags of Spot Wheat Sold

Yesterday, after the futures wheat market opened in the morning, prices for various months did not fluctuate much compared to the closing price of the previous week. As the price of imported wheat only improved by about 0.1-0.2 yuan, both buyers and sellers mostly adopted a wait-and-see attitude. However, prices showed a slightly firm trend amidst the fluctuations. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, due to the improvement in flour prices in the morning and the lack of activity in selling imported wheat, inland groups were ultimately driven by the severity of flood disasters in various places to compete for purchases, causing prices in all sectors to surge again. Although factories sold imported wheat for hedging, the market sentiment remained firm. As a result, the price for this month rose by 0.05 percent compared to the previous week, September/October rose by 0.07 percent, and November/December rose by 0.06 percent. Spot wheat arrivals were insufficient, and inventory was dwindling daily. The combined Shanghai standard price at the place of origin was close to 0.7-0.8 yuan. Therefore, high-quality goods were also quoted at 0.72-0.73 yuan, while medium and lower grades remained flat. Over 13,000 bags of wheat from Penglai, Anqing, Danyang, Qiyan, Zhenjiang, Pudong, Changshu, Taicang, Yangzhou, Shuangfeng, Nanjing, Kunshan, etc., were sold, including 6,000 bags handled by Shenda and Xinda, 4,000 bags handled by Fuxin, and over 3,000 bags handled by Huafeng.

Silk and Tea: Overseas Silk Telegraphs Unchanged 126

Yesterday, the local foreign firm silk market remained sluggish. Overseas silk sales showed no sign of recovery, and silk telegraphs were unchanged yesterday. The market sentiment was depressed. Yesterday, only Weicheng Silk Factory brought in five bales of Shanghai white silk (spot), and Dachang brought in ten bales of white dry silk. Prices remained firm.

New York Raw Silk Consumption Greatly Reduced 127

Totaled Only 40,000+ Bales in July

The United States is the country with the largest consumption of raw silk. New York silk weaving factories are numerous, and the demand for silk is especially strong, requiring 50,000-60,000 bales per month. Since the start of summer, the heat has been unusually high, and silk weaving factories have suspended work, greatly reducing the consumption of raw silk. Last month, countries such as Japan, Italy, and France consumed a total of only 42,500 bales of raw silk, a decrease of nearly 20,000 bales compared to the peak month.

Fine Eyebrow Green Tea Continues to Show a Firm Upward Trend 128

Yesterday, the local foreign firm tea market saw increasing interest in fine eyebrow green teas from Wuyuan and Tunxi, handled by Yongxing, Baochang, Jinlong, Xiehe, and other firms. Overall market trading was unusually brisk, and market prices continued to rise firmly by 0.6-0.7 taels. Foreign tea merchants adopted an increasingly firm attitude due to the limited inventory and sources in the market. Needle eyebrow and Xiumei teas, due to the good prices for tea residue this year in inland areas and the scarcity of supply, are currently in a situation where supply falls short of demand in the market. In addition, for Gongxi tea, the Russian Assistance Association foreign firm resumed inspecting new samples yesterday, preparing to start operations. The green tea market is gradually showing positive signs.

Dried and Preserved Goods: New White Lotus Seeds and Candied Dates Have Arrived 129

The first batch of new white lotus seeds has arrived, and the goods are relatively dry and clean. Yesterday, they were sold at 37 taels, while old goods were sold at 36 taels. Market sentiment was stable. (New candied dates) Yesterday, it was reported that over a dozen barrels of Jiaxing goods had arrived, and sales were expected to start, with a price of 36 taels. Formal Anhui goods would still take time to arrive, and prices would certainly be higher.

Metals: Tinplate Arrivals Exceed 2,000 Boxes Again 130

Metal trading remained flat yesterday, resulting in a lack of major transactions throughout the market, except for a few minor deals. However, in terms of arrivals, another 2,400-2,500 boxes of large and small tinplate arrived yesterday. In terms of prices, there is likely to be no hope of price increases in the future. Currently, American 90-pound goods are estimated at 15.75 taels, and 100-pound goods are estimated at 17 taels. For British goods, 90-pound goods are estimated at 14 taels, 100-pound goods are estimated at 15.5 taels, and 200-pound goods are estimated at 30 taels. Many factories are trading, but customer guild deals are particularly sparse.

French Concession 151

Two Courts Held Office Yesterday 152

Hearing of Eight Criminal Cases

The Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court and the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Local Court both officially began operations yesterday, and at the same time began to add civil and criminal divisions. The Second Special District Local Court then reopened for the first time at noon, hearing eight criminal cases. The details of yesterday's situation are recorded separately below:

Beginning of Operations　The presidents of the two courts ordered all staff to report to the court to sign in and begin work from yesterday.

Court Hearing Cases　Yesterday morning around 10 o'clock, the various criminal cases sent to the Second Special District Local Court by the French Concession Police Department were accepted in the criminal court downstairs at around 12:15 noon. Judge Luo Renji, along with Prosecutor Ding Shikui and Clerk Wang Baoxun, took their seats in the criminal court to hear minor cases, which were completed at 1:15. A total of six theft cases, one opium case, and one kidnapping case requested by the Kunshan authorities were heard. The results were very orderly, and there were many spectators. Judge Luo ordered that the defendants be temporarily detained in the detention center and that a retrial be held on the 18th. As for the requested kidnapping case, it has not yet been transferred because there were no formal official documents and no evidence was presented. It will be transferred once the official documents are received and evidence is presented, it is said.

Continued Appointment of Judges　The Ministry of Judicial Administration continued to appoint personnel to the Higher Third Branch and the Second Special District Local Court in the French Concession of Shanghai as follows: Court Clerks of the Higher Third Branch: Yin Tingxiang, Luo Zonglu, Peng Jianbiao, Qin Shougong, Liu Jiayi, Zhou Che, Shi Ji; Court Clerk of the Prosecutor's Office of the Higher Second Branch: Yao Rongsen; Translator: Peng Wangyong; Court Clerks of the Second Special District Local Court: Zhang JiongGuang, Qian Lisheng, Wu Peihong, Zhu ChaoZhuo, Wu Shan. The Second Special District Court will have one police officer, two police sergeants, six police constables, and sixteen police officers. In accordance with the provisions of item 4 of the agreement, the advisor recommended by the French envoy, now Du Ge, has been recommended and transferred to the court by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for handling. As for the president of the court of the First Special District, Zhou Daren has been appointed, as well as Judges Shen Bingrong, Guo Shouyi, and Li Mo. Zhao Fengxian has also been appointed as the sub-warden of the Shanghai Second Prison, it is said.

Banking Sector

Important Meeting Held Yesterday 153

Regarding the Ministry of Finance's Collection of Paper Money Tax and Income Tax

According to the Huadong News Agency, concerning the Ministry of Finance's plan to levy taxes on the issuance of banknotes and income tax from the banking industry, the banking sector in this city generally believes that this matter is of great importance and has a significant impact on the future of the banking industry. There is also a question of whether Chinese and foreign banks will be taxed equally. Therefore, at 2:00 PM yesterday, a special members' meeting was convened at the clubhouse at No. 4 Hong Kong Road to discuss opinions on this matter. Representatives from all members of the association attended. Mr. Hu Mengjia of the Bank of Communications presided over the meeting and immediately announced the reason for convening the meeting, requesting members to express their opinions on the above two taxes. After a long discussion, it was decided to first solicit the opinions of all member banks. Furthermore, considering that this tax issue concerns the survival of the entire banking industry nationwide, the association also issued notices to banks that have not yet joined the Banking Association, requesting them to conduct thorough research on this matter immediately and submit all opinions to the Banking Association for forwarding to the Ministry of Finance for review and approval. At the same time, telegrams were sent to the Banking Associations in Beiping, Tianjin, Hankou, and other places, urging them to quickly express their opinions on this tax law for mutual reference. The meeting adjourned at approximately 5:00 PM. Regarding this matter, the Huadong News Agency reporter specially visited Mr. Lin Kanghou, a standing committee member of the Banking Association, yesterday to inquire about the opinions of the meeting on the two new taxes. According to Mr. Lin, since the regulations on banknote issuance and income tax were announced, the banking industry has learned that the proponent of this plan was the American advisor to the Ministry of Finance. After the proposal was made, the government naturally welcomed the large tax revenue, as it was legitimate and justified. Chinese bankers, as members of the nation, have no reason to object. However, it is believed that the Chinese banking industry is still in its infancy, and the government is imposing a significant burden on it. There are still several points that raise doubts: First, whether the collection methods for banknote issuance tax and income tax are the same for Chinese and foreign banks, or whether only Chinese banks are subject to the tax while foreign banks are exempt. Second, regarding the general plan for the banknote issuance tax, reports indicate that those with reserves will not be taxed, while those without reserves will be subject to the tax. However, upon investigation, all Chinese and foreign banks do not have a fixed amount of banknote issuance. The nature of banknotes is fluid; one day, ten million may be issued, and the next day, five million may be received. Therefore, does the Ministry of Finance have clear regulations on this point? Third, the nature of income tax is a disguised business tax. The business tax rates in various provinces and cities are calculated in thousandths, but the income tax law promulgated by the national government today stipulates that those with net income below 15% will be taxed at 5%, those with 15% to 25% will be taxed at 7.05%, those with 25% to 35% will be taxed at 10%, and those above 35% will be taxed at 15%. The high tax rate far exceeds the business tax in various provinces and cities. Why does the Ministry of Finance place such a heavy tax burden on the banking industry alone? All these points raise deep concerns among the banking industry. Our country's banking industry has been severely weakened by the oppression and competition from foreign banks. In recent years, people in society have begun to realize the fear of foreign banks' manipulation and have begun to pay attention to our country's banking industry. In recent years, the Chinese banking industry has shown good signs of gradual progress. The government should consider ways to reward and promote it to encourage it. But now, it is not doing so. Moreover, if foreign banks are exclusively exempt, it is tantamount to severely damaging our country's entire banking industry. How can the Chinese banking industry fully develop in the future to compete with foreign banks? Furthermore, it is rumored that this proposal comes from the strategy of the American advisor to the Ministry of Finance. On the surface, it seems to be a good plan for our government, but on the reverse side, the reason for suggesting that the national government collect this regulation is to resist Chinese banks in disguise, so that our immature Chinese banking industry will be hit and give the foreign banks the opportunity to expand as much as possible. Thinking of this, how can we not be afraid? Therefore, the majority of the conference advocated that the Ministry of Finance treat Chinese and foreign banks equally. This is not only for the sake of our country's banking industry itself, but also for the sake of our country's entire financial industry.

No Extension for Registration of Japanese Goods 155

The Anti-Japanese Association and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Both Expressed Their Views

Deadline is the Sixth According to the Resolution

The Anti-Japanese and Aid-Overseas Chinese Committee previously decided at its first executive committee meeting that the deadline for registering purchased Japanese goods would be the 15th, from July 23 to August 6. At the same time, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce held a temporary general meeting of members on the 24th, and it was also decided to conduct a registration of Japanese goods in member stores, with a two-week deadline, from the 24th to August 6 as well. It is reported that a large number of people have gone to register in recent days. The association issued announcements and letters yesterday, stating that the registration deadline would not be extended. The original text is recorded as follows:

Announcement of the Anti-Japanese Association The Anti-Japanese Association issued its eighth announcement yesterday, stating: The registration of Japanese goods by our association will end on the 6th of this month according to the resolution of the Executive Committee. It is hoped that all merchants and citizens in the city will come to the association before the deadline to register their accumulated Japanese goods in accordance with the regulations. Do not delay yourselves. This is very important.

Reply from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce The Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied to the South Goods Trade Association yesterday, stating: Reply to your letter requesting that the Anti-Japanese Association extend the deadline for registering Japanese goods and exempt payment of relief funds. The registration deadline was decided by the temporary meeting of members of our association on July 27 and cannot be extended. As for the relief fund measures, according to the resolution of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese and Aid-Overseas Chinese Committee, it is only collected for Japanese goods purchased and paid for with silver after the 14th and before the 24th, not for all Japanese goods. Collection must be made, and the association has already announced this in the newspaper. The requests in your letter seem difficult to accommodate. Please check and inform.

Announcement of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Do Not Raise the Price of Domestic Goods 156

Resisting Japanese Goods is a Good Opportunity to Promote Domestic Goods

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce notified the trade associations of all industries yesterday, stating: According to a letter from the Shanghai Anti-Japanese and Aid-Overseas Chinese Committee, on the 28th of this month, the printing industry labor union sent a letter requesting restrictions on the opportunistic price increases of domestic goods to benefit the people's livelihood. At this time of national economic severance with Japan, it is the only time to widely consume domestic goods. However, a few merchants often take the opportunity to raise prices, losing the public's faith in purchasing for small profits, which is deeply regrettable. According to the letter, the above situation should be informed and checked. Approved. The whole city is now enthusiastically resisting Japanese goods, which is indeed a good opportunity to promote domestic goods. It is appropriate to have fair prices to stimulate public interest in purchasing. Do not raise prices as a result, which may cause repercussions. According to the letter, corresponding notices are hereby given, and all members are requested to check, inform, and comply.

Japanese Merchant Customs Brokerage

Taking the Opportunity to Solicit the Declaration and Loading of Japanese Goods 157

Chinese Customs Brokerage Houses Are Greatly Panicked

However, They Still Refuse to Load and Await Government Prohibition

After the Shanghai Anti-Japanese and Aid-Overseas Chinese Association implemented economic severance with Japan, the transshipment and customs declaration industry has implemented automatic refusal to load Japanese goods. In order to prevent Japanese customs brokerage houses from taking the opportunity to contract loading and transportation, a request was submitted to the authorities for prohibition. Unexpectedly, Japanese customs brokerage houses such as Higuchi, Yamaguchi, and Yiji sent personnel to contract the loading and transportation of Japanese goods separately, and they even contained insurance. There are even newly opened Japanese customs brokerage houses specializing in the declaration of Japanese goods, causing more than 800 Chinese customs brokerage houses, such as Yuanfeng and Kunk, to panic. However, in order to implement the spirit of patriotism, they have no choice but to wait for the authorities to take measures to prohibit them. Yesterday, the association received an instruction from the Municipal Party Department, which read: According to the report for prohibiting Japanese customs brokerage houses to facilitate commercial transportation, the request has been forwarded to the central government for approval. Please comply.

Wang Zhengting's Reply to Yu Qiaqing's Letter 158

I Will Still Work Hard While in Office

Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting replied to Yu Qiaqing's letter, stating: Dear Elder Brother Qia Lao, I received your frugal telegram. Your words are earnest and sincere. After reading it respectfully, I am filled with shame and gratitude. The Chairman often tells the people that the responsibility of office is to fulfill obligations, not to enjoy rights. I have followed the Premier for many years and have always taken revolution as my ambition. I regard the affairs of the party and the country as our duty. Therefore, since taking office, I have been dedicated and tireless, and I do not complain. You, my brother, know this well. When the Korean massacre occurred, it was my duty to work hard. I also wish to be no less patriotic than others. However, people's opinions differ. I try my best to fulfill my obligations, but others may see them as rights. If it is a matter of rights, I can immediately resign to give way to the capable. This is the reason for my resolute request for resignation this time. Since I am encouraged by righteousness, I dare not refuse. While in office, I will continue to work hard to fulfill my responsibilities. I hope you will understand my foolishness. I send this telegram to thank you and wish you well. Your younger brother Wang Zhengting.

Hengtong Steamer Sinks in Shaobo 161

Crew Safe

The China Merchants Inland River Shipping Bureau's Zhenjiang-Yangzhou steamer Hengtong was ordered to sail during the suspension of service in Yangzhou. When it was near Shaobo, the ship crashed and sank immediately. All the crew members escaped from the water. The loss was huge. The report was received in Shanghai yesterday. The situation is recorded as follows:

Adventurous Departure The twenty-six routes of the China Merchants Inland River Shipping Bureau's steamers were all suspended due to the major flood disaster last month. The Zhenjiang-Yangzhou steamer Hengtong was suspended in Yangzhou from July 15. On July 28, the steamer was suddenly ordered to go to Qingjiangpu, towing four civilian boats in Yangzhou, and had to set off immediately. At that time, the director of the Yangzhou branch and the captain of the ship both said that the water was high along the way and the voyage was dangerous and could not be carried out. However, the negotiations were unsuccessful, and the shipowners had no choice but to start from Yangzhou, towing the four civilian boats, and taking the risk to Qingjiangpu.

Accident on the Way The water along the way was extremely high, and the farmland on both sides was flooded. Navigation was very difficult. The shipowner drove slowly to avoid collision and prevent farmers from obstructing navigation and sabotage. That night, when it was about ten miles away from Shaobo's Bihuba, it was already dark, and the water was turbulent and extremely dangerous. The shipowner thought that it could not be opened any more, and he wanted to stop sailing and wait for the next day to drive after dawn. Unexpectedly, this aroused the anger of the escorts, who whipped and forced the shipowner to drive. One crew member was beaten and injured and did not dare to disobey. So they negotiated to change the tow twice. Because of the high tide and rapid current of Bihuba, they were afraid that all four ships would be overturned. After negotiation, Hengtong first towed two ships, and in the dark, they rushed through the dangerous area with the current and arrived at Shaobo.

Ship Sinks The first time was a fluke success at great risk. The second time, Hengtong went to Bihuba again to tow the boat. It was already late at night, and the water flow was even more fierce. When it was about to reach the civilian boat, the person on the boat ordered to advance quickly. As a result, the bottom of the Hengtong ship crashed into a large iron anchor on the civilian boat parked on the dam shore. The anchor tip broke the bottom of the wheel, and the river water poured into the wheel frantically. In a short time, the wheel body was submerged in the river. Dozens of people on the wheel luckily jumped into the civilian boat to avoid danger, while the crew members jumped into the water one after another and fled to the shore. They were also afraid that the wheel would be washed away by the flood. Fortunately, the shipowner tied the rope to the deck on the shore in a hurry. Therefore, although the wheel was completely submerged, it was still on the river bank. All public and private items were completely submerged in the wheel and could not be taken out. The loss amounted to tens of thousands of yuan.

Send Someone to Investigate Thoroughly Yesterday, the Shanghai Bureau received a report and immediately sent staff member Bai Gongbi, who was dispatched by Manager Zhang Jingpei, to Yangzhou to conduct an on-the-spot investigation and verify whether the wheel had any hope of being towed and rescued, because the Hengtong wheel was the best steamer of the China Merchants Inland River Shipping Bureau. The crew members who escaped have returned to Yangzhou to report to the branch. Yesterday, the Shanghai Bureau reported the Hengtong wheel accident to the Zhejiang Construction Department through the Secretariat, and requested that the Ministry of Communications be notified that no risky forced departures should be made during the flood period.

A Cry for Flood Relief 162

Disaster Reports Received by Various Groups

Red Cross Society The Chinese Red Cross Society received three important telegrams yesterday: 1. Wei Ruifeng and Wu Jiasan, special disaster investigators sent by the Red Cross Society to Jiangxi, telegraphed: Jiangxi Province has been suffering from continuous rain in recent days. Low-lying areas have become swamps due to flash floods, with Yongxiu, De'an, Jiujiang, Hukou, Fengcheng, Xingan, and Xiajiang being the most severely affected. Other areas such as Ji'an, Anfu, and Wan'an are also suffering from heavy rain. Most of the crops have been submerged. After suffering from the communist disaster first, they are now suffering from natural disasters again. For days, wired communication has been blocked by water, and wireless communication has been temporarily suspended due to military use. The Nanxun Road has also been blocked by water, making reporting extremely difficult. This telegram was sent by Commander Xiong on behalf of the investigators. 2. The Wanzhizhen Chamber of Commerce telegraphed: From the 20th of this month, the Qingyi River Basin has been experiencing torrential rain. On the 2nd, mountain floods broke out suddenly and poured down directly, coupled with the backflow of the river tide, the water volume increased repeatedly, resulting in the successive collapse of more than 40 embankments, especially on the afternoon of the 25th, the western part of the town was the most tragic, with more than half of the people and houses dead, injured, and washed away. The cries of the hungry and displaced can be heard everywhere, and the corpses are all over the river. Currently, there are 200,000 disaster victims waiting to be rescued. 3. The Yingshang Red Cross Society telegraphed: This time, the Huai and Ying rivers overflowed, and the flood disaster suffered by our county is greater than that of the tenth year of the Republic of China and heavier than that of Fuyang. Tens of thousands of houses have been submerged and collapsed, and the number of floating firewood, drowned people and animals is countless.

Chinese and Foreign Relief Society The Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Society received a letter from the Finance Bureau of Tongcheng County, Anhui Province, stating: Our hometown is adjacent to the river and lake, and the land is the lowest-lying, relying entirely on embankments to block the water. This year, the spring flood broke out, and the river tide was full early. Unexpectedly, the recent heavy rain has been torrential for five days without stopping, and dozens of embankment collapses have been connected. Seeing the disaster victims, it is very pitiful. Our bureau has organized an emergency relief committee in advance, but a drop in the bucket is of no avail. I especially send a telegram to appeal, and I implore you to directly grant relief funds, awaiting orders. Also, a telegram from various institutions and groups in Hexian County stated: Hexian County has suffered from soldiers, bandits, locusts, and droughts in recent years, and the suffering of the people is indescribable. But the sky has not ended the disaster, and the people are still suffering. First, there was continuous spring rain, and recently there has been heavy rain, resulting in mountain floods and sudden rises in the river tide. All the weirs have become swamps. Some farmland, rice fields, and houses have been washed away, and some people have been drowned. The whole area is desolate, and life is almost extinct. What will be the solution to the aftermath? I think your association is concerned about the suffering of the people and is meticulous. I especially submit the disaster situation and give relief. Also, a public letter from the Jiangpu County Government of Jiangsu Province stated that unfortunately, since July, there has been continuous heavy rain and flash floods. The seedlings have rotted, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. The water depth in the plains is several feet, and all the houses, livestock, and furniture have been lost. Many people have died due to the sudden flood and the inability to avoid it. At present, the victims have nowhere to live and no food to eat. Please give relief quickly. Also, a telegram from the Jiangning County Government of Jiangsu Province stated that there has been continuous heavy rain in our county, and mountain floods have broken out. 70 to 80 percent of the large and small dikes in the county have been submerged and collapsed, and those that have not collapsed are still in danger. Farmland and houses are almost submerged. The Jinghu Line, from Yaohuamen to Hepingmen, is particularly overflowing with water, with several feet of water and a vast ocean along the line. The victims are displaced, eating and sleeping in the open, and the situation is extremely miserable. The situation is unbearable to see. Now the transportation of the whole county is completely blocked. The disaster is so severe that it has not been seen in decades. Please provide relief. Also, a telegram from the Provisional Flood Relief Committee of Quanjiao County, Anhui stated that the flood disaster in Quanjiao is extremely severe. The provincial government has allocated 2,000 yuan for emergency relief, which is being distributed. Heavy rain for two days and nights, and the flood rushed urgently, and countless people and animals were drowned. The cries of the victims are unbearable to hear. The weirs have long been broken, and the mountain fields have been completely submerged. The autumn harvest is hopeless. The conference decided to temporarily move the relief funds for distribution. Please send someone to investigate and quickly allocate emergency relief to save the victims.

Anhui Fellow Association This summer, there has been heavy rain and disaster. Except for the mountain counties, the remaining counties along the river and Huai River in Anhui Province have been flooded and have become disaster areas. The Anhui Fellow Association in this port has received telegrams requesting relief like snowflakes. The misery of the disaster is difficult to describe. In recent days, the association's staff has been discussing and convening an emergency meeting of all directors and supervisors to organize the Anhui Flood Relief Association, dividing it into three departments: fundraising, writing and art. The three departments will proceed together. The calligraphy and painting department invites famous calligraphers and painters from Anhui, such as Xu Jingren, Xu Jilong, Huang Binhong, Wang Juyou, and Xu Shiqi, to take on the task, and all proceeds will be used to help relieve the disaster. Here is a record of the reply telegram from the National Government Relief Committee and the Anhui Provincial Government: 1. According to the Chairman's delegation, your association respectfully telegraphed that the counties along the river and Huai River in this province are suffering from heavy rain and disaster, which is an unprecedented catastrophe. You have described the situation in detail, requesting that the national treasury be issued quickly for emergency relief and that labor relief be arranged to guide the Huai River, and that the provincial government be ordered to rush to repair the dikes along the river. The instructions have been delegated to the Executive Yuan, etc. In addition to sending a letter, corresponding letters are issued for reference. National Government Civil Service Office. 2. Approved and respectfully delegated telegrams that according to the reports from the counties bordering the Jiang and Huai Rivers in Anhui Province, the flood disaster is severe and it is requested that the national treasury be issued quickly for emergency relief. The Anhui disaster is severe, and reports have been received from various parties, which is deeply sad. However, in recent years, various provinces have submitted reports of flood disasters, and letters and telegrams have been sent one after another requesting relief. The association is now doing its best to plan and submit it to the Executive Yuan for the issuance of large sums of money for relief. Once the fundraising is completed, a meeting will be held to discuss the allocation separately. Special telegram reply, Relief Committee. 3. Respectfully and diligently read the telegram. The counties in this province bordering the Jiang and Huai Rivers have been severely flooded, and the county governments have successively submitted reports to the government, and each has been ordered to properly appease and relieve the disaster and allocate 1,200 yuan for emergency relief. However, due to the province's odd shortage and the heavy disaster, the government has repeatedly telegraphed the National Government Executive Yuan and Relief Committee to quickly allocate large sums of money for relief, which is on file. However, considering that the disaster situation in each county is extremely severe, and the difficulties of the time cannot be remedied without concerted efforts. I hope that your association will embrace the people of the same race and do your best to persuade and raise funds to save the drowning and hunger together. The Anhui Provincial Government seals the world.

A Cry After the Summer Rain Disaster 163

The Agricultural Association Pours Out Grievances of Crop Failure, Requesting Tax Exemption

The Shanghai County Agricultural Association submitted a document to the County Government yesterday, stating: "Regarding the request, the agricultural associations of the First Township, Fourth District, and other townships reported that since the beginning of the month, there have been continuous torrential rains. During this period of intense heat, the river water has risen sharply, and low-lying fields are flooded with ankle-deep water, unable to drain. Cotton seedlings are rotting at the roots, and they are vulnerable to withering in the sudden intense sunlight. Although high-lying fields are not flooded, the prolonged overcast skies have prevented sunlight, causing the seedlings to sprout and become as tender as vegetables, with no flower buds at all. The rice seedlings are about to produce weeds. This heavy rain and strong wind have destroyed most of them, making it difficult to yield a harvest. As for beans, melons, fruits, vegetables, and other developed agricultural products, many have suffered leaf blight and withered, making it difficult to thrive. At a time when the country is in turmoil, with continuous warfare, farmers have suffered repeated disasters. Taxes are heavy, and prices are high. Even the various trades and crafts rely on agriculture. A full harvest every year already feels like a heavy burden. Now, suddenly faced with this natural disaster, the autumn harvest is bound to be disappointing. Our association is deeply concerned but lacks the means to remedy the situation. The public is panicking and strongly appeals for help. Therefore, we specially request your esteemed association to send personnel to investigate the situation on the ground and report the disaster to the County Government, who in turn should request the Provincial Government to devise a method of assistance. We sincerely hope you will consider this matter." Upon receiving this, it was found that the widespread rain disaster affected a large area. Although the county is located near the coast and has not immediately become a swamp, the impact on the young crops, which are crucial for yielding a harvest, is significant. At a time when the people are impoverished and resources are exhausted, the lives of farmers are such that many do not have enough grain to eat from one morning to the next, and they resort to pawning and borrowing, living hand to mouth. A good harvest year is already a struggle to sustain themselves, and facing a famine, they will inevitably cry out in hunger and cold. In accordance with the previous report, special personnel were repeatedly dispatched to the countryside to investigate the disaster, and the report was found to be accurate. Therefore, we have prepared a document to submit to your esteemed office, requesting that you promptly telegraph the Provincial Government to ask for a reduction or exemption of taxes to provide relief, which would be in the public interest.

The Grain Committee Requests to Hold a Food Exhibition 164

As a Prelude to Comprehensively Solving the People's Food Problem

The Municipal Grain Committee believes that the public's food panic is worsening year by year, and this year, with frequent floods, signs of famine are already apparent. To address both the symptoms and the root cause, it is necessary to implement separate measures. It has already submitted a request to the central government to organize a food exhibition, which has been approved and forwarded. The content is as follows:

Reasons for holding the exhibition (omitted above): In recent years, national affairs have been tumultuous, and the people's livelihood has been exhausted. Foreign aggression has not ceased, and banditry in the hinterland still exists. The price of silver has plummeted, and foreign goods are dumped into the market, devastating industry and commerce. Agricultural products are also declining daily. Each year, food imports, considering only rice, wheat, and flour, already amount to about 200 million yuan. If we include seafood, livestock products, and canned foods, the total is over 300 million yuan. It is thought that the amount of imports over exports of our country in recent years is about 200 million taels of customs silver, which is equivalent to about 300 million yuan in national currency. If there were no such huge imports of food products, then our country could maintain a balanced state in international trade. Now, a country known to the world as an agricultural nation is in such a state. What is its impact on the people's livelihood? What is its impact on the national economy? It is a great shame for our nation and a great crisis for our country. From this perspective, the people's livelihood problem and the national economy problem are also the food problem. Therefore, the most urgent task at present is to encourage production and improve distribution. Increased production will ensure sufficient food for the people, and equitable distribution will stabilize grain prices. With sufficient food and stable prices, the people's hardship will be alleviated. As for increasing production and improving distribution, it is important to have on-site guidance and research to achieve practical results. Promotion and observation are particularly sufficient to encourage the people, so that they know to be vigilant and think of self-help. This committee believes that the planning of the food exhibition cannot be delayed. (1) Although the country has felt the pain of food shortages in recent years, it is not yet clear about the reality of insufficient production. For example, how much does a certain province produce? How much does a certain province consume? Which provinces have a shortage, and which have a surplus? What is the state of food imports and exports? How are agricultural products distributed? All of this requires collecting detailed statistics for observation. (2) Domestic agricultural, animal husbandry, aquatic products, and other stable food cultivation, breeding, processing, and manufacturing industries have made considerable progress. However, compared with foreign countries, how large is the difference? What are the shortcomings? It is also necessary to collect materials for practical research and theoretical discussions for social reference and to promote the improvement of various industries. (3) Food is an indispensable element of life. Knowledge about food, such as rice polishing methods, cooking skills, portion sizes, and nutritional value, should be comparatively studied to instill common sense in the people, increase national health, and improve family finances. (4) Domestic research materials on food are inevitably fragmented. Although there are many rich knowledge and academic studies that can be treasured,

Organization of the Preparatory Committee: (1) Organization: The central government will set up a preparatory committee to carry out the work, and the relevant government departments at home and abroad will assist and divide the work. Each department should also set up a special committee, and the detailed measures will be formulated separately. (2) Exhibits: All exhibits should be scientific so that visitors can obtain various knowledge and interests. (3) Funding: Assuming 500,000 yuan, the central government will allocate 300,000 yuan, and each province and city will share 5,000 yuan. The shortfall will be covered by admission fees, advertising fees, and merchandise display fees. (4) Preparation period: It is planned for one year.

Classification of Exhibits: Category 1: Food and Life Department. (Content:) Includes the relationship between life and food, body nutrition, dietary hygiene, etc. (Purpose:) To enlighten each person about the necessary knowledge of diet to enhance health care, infant care, and elderly care methods, and to promote society to choose nutritious, beneficial, and hygienic foods. (Topics omitted) Category 2: Population and Food Problem Department. (Content:) The trend of population growth and the relationship with food production and supply, birth control, immigration, and border colonization methods. (Purpose:) To arouse social awareness of the dangers of world population growth and the decline of our nation, the large-scale import of food each year, and the phenomenon of declining domestic production, so that they can be alert, and to imply the feasibility of birth control and the necessity of immigration and border colonization. (Topics omitted) Category 3: Agricultural Food Department. (Content:) The current status of various agricultural productions in China and the necessity of agricultural improvement issues. (Purpose:) To arouse social awareness of the relationship between agriculture and people's livelihood and to understand the relationship between Chinese agriculture and world demand and supply. (Topics omitted) Category 4: Aquatic and Animal Food Department. (Content:) The current status of domestic aquatic and livestock breeding and the import and export of various aquatic and livestock products. (Purpose:) To arouse social awareness of aquatic and livestock products, and at the same time to promote aquaculture, promote milk, improve chicken farming, and egg products. (Topics omitted) Category 5: Processing and Storage Department. (Content:) The processing and storage of various agricultural, livestock, and aquatic products, as well as cooking methods, and the comparison of various storage methods. (Purpose:) Regarding the production and consumption of processed products, the improvement of food cooking and storage methods. (Topics omitted) Category 6: Distribution and Consumption Department. (Content:) The supply, distribution, and consumption of various foods and their methods. (Purpose:) Seeking the rationalization of supply, distribution, and consumption. (Topics omitted) Category 7: Publicity and Lecture Department. (Content:) A lecture hall is set up for tourists to rest and for internal publicity. (Purpose:) To increase the knowledge of visitors. (Topics omitted)

Order from the Social Affairs Bureau

Approval of Women's Working Hours 165

Article 13 of the Factory Law

A Two-Year Preparation Period

After the promulgation of the Factory Law, the implementation was postponed to August 1st. Various factories have requested a postponement of Article 13 of the Factory Law, which stipulates that women shall not work between 10 PM and 6 AM the next morning. It is now heard that the Labor Department of the Ministry of Industry telegraphed the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, stating: "Regarding the request to postpone Article 13 of the Factory Law, this Ministry has forwarded it to the Executive Yuan for review. The State Council then decided to submit it to the Political Council for approval. On the 29th of this month (July), the Central Political Council decided that Article 13 of the Factory Law shall be granted a two-year preparation period for implementation, under the supervision of the Ministry of Industry. This is specially telegraphed." It is heard that the bureau has informed the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the National Goods Factory Federation, and the Machine-Made National Goods Factory Federation to inform the various factories.

The Printing Industry Suspended Operations Yesterday 166

Union Director Wang Xingquan Arrested and Released

Due to the implementation of the Factory Law regulations, workers in the Shanghai printing industry, in order to comply with the law, suddenly and voluntarily switched to an eight-hour workday starting on August 1st. The Printing Industry Guild, finding it difficult to maintain operations, decided at a general meeting to temporarily suspend operations starting yesterday. The details are as follows:

Notice of Suspension: The Printing Industry Guild notified all members the night before to suspend operations together, stating: "Regarding the notice, workers in this industry suddenly and voluntarily implemented an eight-hour workday on August 1st. This guild convened an emergency meeting of all members yesterday afternoon at 6 PM to discuss solutions. It was generally believed that the members of this guild have been repeatedly oppressed by the labor union and are unable to maintain operations. It was decided that all members will reluctantly suspend operations together this Monday and send representatives to petition the Social Affairs Bureau on Monday morning to preside over the matter and then resume operations. We must persevere to the end and take unified action. A meeting of members will be held at 2 PM on Monday afternoon to discuss solutions. Your presence is essential. This is a special notice."

Labor and Management Petition: The Printing Industry Labor Union sent Xia Hailin and Wang Xingquan to the Social Affairs Bureau at 9 AM yesterday to petition, requesting: (1) Strictly order the employers to resume operations and restore the workers' jobs; (2) Punish the Printing Industry Guild, which instigated the suspension of operations; (3) Expedite the mediation of treatment conditions. The bureau director Zhang Shuye accepted the requests. The Printing Industry Guild also sent Zhu Kejun, Zhang Yixin, Wang Wenxian, Dai Zhonglin, and six others to the Social Affairs Bureau at 10 AM yesterday to petition, requesting: (1) Strictly prohibit the labor union from taking free action; (2) Restore the original nine-hour workday to maintain business difficulties. Bureau director Zhang Shuye also accepted the requests.

Director Arrested: After the guild announced the suspension of operations, more than 30 companies, including Meisheng, Liangyang, and Huayang, suspended operations together yesterday morning, and some, such as Dongxing Laoyishun, expelled workers. Upon learning of this, the Printing Industry Labor Union immediately sent standing committee members Xia Hailin and Wang Xingquan to persuade the workers to strictly observe order and not take extreme actions. At the same time, they demanded that the employers resume operations. When they arrived at Dongxing Printing on Beijing Road, they were reported to the police, resulting in the arrest of union director Wang Xingquan and taken to the Fuzhou Road police station. After questioning by the police chief, he was released because he had not disturbed public order.

Emergency Meeting: The Printing Industry Guild held an emergency meeting of members at 2 PM yesterday. Chairman Zhu Kejun reported on the wishful process and the suspension of operations. The following resolutions were unanimously adopted on the spot: (1) If the workers do not restore the nine-hour workday, the industry will resolutely suspend operations together; (2) Continue to submit a statement to the Social Affairs Bureau explaining the hardship; (3) Send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and various industry guilds requesting assistance; (4) An emergency meeting will be held at 7 PM at 4 PM.

Order from the Social Affairs Bureau: After receiving petitions from both labor and management in the printing industry yesterday, the Social Affairs Bureau believed that it was inappropriate for the workers to voluntarily implement an eight-hour workday and that the employers' unauthorized suspension of operations was also rash. It strictly ordered both labor and management to resume work as usual within the stipulated time limit and await review.

Union Declaration: The Shanghai Printing Industry Labor Union declares on the illegal suspension of operations by employers: "All labor groups are aware that the labor-management contract of our union has been signed for nearly two years. According to government regulations, it can be amended after a full year. Our union is for labor-management cooperation, seeking its realization from theory. Although prices have increased and workers' lives are difficult, all workers can still serve with peace of mind. Their consideration for the employers' situation is not inconsiderable, and their commitment to the development of business is not insincere. This time, our union proposed to amend the contract based on the principle of reasonableness, and all the articles were approved by the Municipal Party Department. Our union immediately requested the employers to negotiate. The letter was sent seven times, but the employers ignored it. On August 3rd, the Printing Industry Guild convened a meeting of all members and ordered the industry to illegally suspend operations, expel all workers, seal the factory, and stop providing food and lodging, creating a disturbance. They also used the power of the concession to arrest innocent workers and imprison them. The various situations show that the guild intentionally oppresses the workers and destroys the labor movement, which is undeniable. However, in addition to making a final effort to deal with the employers' unreasonable oppression, we sincerely hope that all labor groups in the city will give sympathetic assistance. This is a declaration."

Liang Chengyu Again 169

Accused of Being the Leader of a Kidnapping Case 170

Two Accomplices Came Forward to Accuse Him

The Police Station Asks for a Special Re-Examination

Liang Chengyu, a Shandong native who previously served as a Chinese detective at the General Inspection Office, was brought to the Special District Court in connection with the robbery of morphine from Fang Liansheng (also known as Xiao Liansheng Li Liansheng), but he was acquitted due to insufficient evidence. The police station's lawyer, Ru Bao-yi, filed an appeal to the High Court, which ordered a retrial. All details have been reported previously. Fang Liansheng and Lu A-gen, Hu A-long, etc., kidnapped Chen Shi-fan on Pingwang Street on the evening of December 19th last year at around 9 PM, and kidnapped Li Hui-qing on Guangxi Road on the early morning of February 8th this year at around 1 AM, obtaining 7,000 yuan. After the case was discovered, they were brought to the Special Court for questioning. Lu A-gen was sentenced to death, Fang Liansheng was sentenced to life imprisonment, and Hu A-long was sentenced to 20 years in prison. Now, Lu and Fang have confessed that Liang Chengyu was actually the leader of the two kidnapping cases. The police station added the kidnapping charge against Liang in the Special Court. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao Xie-fen attended the third courtroom for questioning. According to the police station representative, lawyer Li Zhi-shan, who explained the case and said that the two witness prisoners, Lu A-gen and Fang Liansheng, had not yet arrived to testify, he requested an extension for a special re-examination. When Liang Chengyu was questioned, he claimed that he did not know Lu A-gen at all. He knew Fang Liansheng for about four or five months and often met him on South Chengdu Road, but they did not greet each other. I was promoted to detective at the police station for more than a year. He also hired lawyers Ye Fo-kang and Yuan Yang-an to briefly argue the case. Judge Xiao ruled that he should be remanded in custody and rescheduled for a special examination.

Using the Chairman's Name to Extort a Bribe

Received Several Contacts

Only Fang Yue-shan Was Caught

Zhang Zhi-xiang, a Ningbo native who owns the Jintai Customs Brokerage Firm at No. 91 Gongshun Lane, Guangdong Road, suddenly received a threatening letter on the 27th of last month, bearing the name of Chairman Wang Chong-fei, intending to extort 3,000 yuan in foreign currency. It instructed him to book a room at the Zhongnan Hotel on the afternoon of the 29th at 7:30 PM and have Director Fang come to negotiate, but the name Li Tian-sheng must be written on the door. Zhang immediately reported to the General Patrol House. The chief ordered Chinese detectives Geng De-biao, Bao detective Tian Jin-fu, Ma Wen-da, and Sun Ai-zhong to go to Room 205 of the Zhongnan Hotel to wait, but no representative from the gang arrived. They had to return to report. By the morning of the 31st, Zhang received another letter, asking him to negotiate at the entrance of the Xiaoshijie Second Bookstore at 7 PM. Zhang reported to the police again. Geng detective and others still went, and Tian detective acted as Zhang's representative. Before long, a Qingpu native named Fang Yue-shan came and invited Tian detective to the roof to talk. Tian immediately told him that Zhang's finances were not very good, so he could not obey the order and could only offer 500 yuan, but Fang refused, saying that he needed to ask for instructions from the chairman. He made an appointment to meet at the Far East Hotel the next day (August 1st). The name Li Tian-sheng still had to be written on the sign. Tian detective agreed. The next morning, two rooms, 503 and 504, were opened in the Far East Hotel to wait for Fang to come and be arrested. At 11 o'clock, they suddenly received a call from Fang, saying that the Far East Hotel was inconvenient and asked them to go to Xiaoshijie. The detectives went immediately and found Fang there. They immediately arrested him and took him back to the police station. Under questioning, it was learned that there was an accomplice named Qi Zi-qing at No. 20 Shengyuan Road. The detectives went to arrest him but found no one. Yesterday morning, Fang was sent to the First Criminal Court of the Special District Court. Chief Judge Zhou Han-ting took the seat for questioning. According to the police station lawyer Ru Bao-yi, who explained the case and said that the case should be rescheduled for questioning after the interrogation, because the defendant had previously committed crimes such as robbery, theft, and carrying firearms, and had been sentenced to imprisonment by the court, it was necessary to investigate whether he had committed other crimes. When the defendant was questioned, he claimed that he was fooled by Qi. Judge Zhou then ordered a rescheduling of the interrogation.

Expands the Subject Matter of the Property Division 171

From 200,000 Yuan to 500,000 Yuan

The statement roughly stated: "As for the case of Yi-gu and others regarding the inheritance and division of the estate with Xue Sun and others, the subject matter of the lawsuit was temporarily set at 200,000 yuan because the estate could not be determined at that time. The petitioners have now learned that the property left by their late maternal grandfather, Mr. Xue Bao-run, such as shares and real estate, is of great value. Although there is no definite figure, according to the market price, it should be at least 3 million yuan. And various deposits are not included. According to one-sixth calculation, the petitioners should get at least 500,000 yuan. The court fees for this expanded subject matter are very high. The petitioners are still minors and have no ability to live. The legal guardian has recently lost his job. The last time he raised money for the petitioners to pay for the lawsuit, he was exhausted. Therefore, we ask the court to approve the expansion of the subject matter of the lawsuit to a total of 500,000 yuan, and to grant litigation assistance for the court costs for the expanded portion. As for the security deposit stipulated in Article 18 of the revised litigation fee rules, it should be added. The combination declaration is made." Yesterday morning, Judge Li Mo of the Special Court attended the ninth civil court for questioning. Chunjiang Wharf

Dispute Between Two Gangs of Workers 172

Originated from the Struggle for Wharf Business

Fortunately, Strict Precautions Prevented Accidents

Along the Pudong Yanpu area, there are many ports and complex workers. The struggle for wharf business is often heard. Recently, for example, a case involving Hubei workers fighting over the foreman position at the Hongsheng Wharf has not yet been resolved. However, two gangs of workers at the Yongchang Wharf in Chunjiang Wharf, Lujiazui, have been plotting to seize the foreman position for days. Although the local military police have taken strict precautions, no violent incidents have occurred. However, the wharf has temporarily suspended operations, awaiting resolution from the superiors. The details of the investigation are recorded below.

Report from the Shandong Gang: The Third District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau received a report from Wang Zhao-qi, the foreman of the Shandong gang, the night before, stating that there is a machine room next to the Rihua Cotton Mill at Chunjiang Wharf, which was originally the property of the Best Times Foreign Firm, specializing in stacking cowhide and other goods. Later, it was purchased by the Hexing Company and leased to Yongchang Wharf to stack miscellaneous grains. It started business on the 31st of last month. The director of the wharf, Chai Kang-qin, hired Min as the foreman and established a guarantee, with a contract. However, at 2 PM on the 1st of this month, Min continued to lead more than 30 workers into the wharf to work. Unexpectedly, a Hubei man named Hu Lao-er brought more than 100 Hubei workers, with a fierce momentum. Without asking the reason, they drove the original workers out of the wharf and forcibly took over the work. Therefore, he reported to the wharf owner and temporarily suspended operations, requesting fairness to maintain labor movement.

The Barbarity of the Hubei Gang: District Chief Zhang, considering the matter related to local peace and order, sent a police officer to patrol in rotation every day to prevent fighting. On the one hand, he summoned the wharf owner Chai Kang-qin to inquire about the cause of the dispute. It was actually caused by the unreasonable behavior of Hu Lao-er, the Hubei foreman. Therefore, at 8 AM yesterday morning, he ordered the police to summon Hu for questioning.

Both Sides Transferred to the Headquarters: According to Hu, he is from Huangpi, Hubei, and has been a wharf foreman for many years. The wharf is located in the Chunjiang Wharf section, which is within his working range. Wang Zhao-qi's workplace is in the Lujiazui area and cannot allow him to overstep. When the district chief asked Hu what evidence he had, Hu was vague. It was decided to transfer both sides to the headquarters for disposal. The wharf remained closed yesterday, awaiting resolution from the superiors.

French Sailor

Fell into the Mingyuan Swimming Pool 173

Died Suddenly from a Heart Attack

The North-China Daily News reported that on Sunday, a French warship sailor, Gus, was at the edge of the Mingyuan Swimming Pool, preparing to jump in for a swim, when he collapsed into the pool, presumably due to heatstroke. He was rescued and sent to the hospital. After examination by a doctor, it was said that he died suddenly from a heart attack. No water was found in his lungs. It is reported that the Mingyuan Swimming Pool had even more visitors yesterday afternoon than on the opening night on Thursday. The pool was full of people. The park manager hired a team of lifeguards. When they saw someone who was not good at swimming venturing into the deep water, they immediately went to help. Gus was preparing to jump into the pool when he suddenly fell. The lifeguards immediately swam to rescue him. However, the place where he fell was 13 feet deep, and his body was tightly against the pool wall. New York Shanghai Stock Fluctuation News 174

The New York Eastern Bank in this city has compiled a table on the average prices of 20 important Shanghai stocks. The average price in January of this year was 24.20, and the average price on July 25 was 27.07, an increase of 2.97 points in seven months, accounting for more than 12 percent. The increase was especially large from January 22 to February 21, 1930, from 24.25 to 27.29. The highest in April reached 27.48. The sixth and seventh months also saw an upward trend. At that time, the market prices of exchanges in various countries were trending downward. This is all due to economic relations, so this table is very useful for merchants to refer to. Researchers of world events, after observing that the market prices of exchanges in various countries fell after the announcement of the US President Hoover's plan to suspend war debt payments, while the Shanghai market prices rose instead, this is also worth noting.

Wusong District

Slight Reduction in Rickshaw and Small Cart Tax Rates 176

Since the Wusong district was placed under the jurisdiction of this city, all vehicles should obtain municipal government licenses, and the vehicle tax should be collected by the municipal government, consistent with other districts. It is understood that the Finance and Public Works Bureaus, considering that the Wusong market is not yet fully developed, took this into account when formulating the tax rates. However, given that Wusong is also within the municipal area, consistent tax collection is appropriate to avoid discrimination. Furthermore, Wusong is adjacent to the northern districts of the city, and vehicles that have paid the tax can operate in the southern and northern parts of the city. Considering that the number of rickshaws in the southern and northern parts of the city is already at its limit, without any further increases allowed, Wusong rickshaws have the opportunity to operate throughout the city, which is not without benefit. Therefore, it was submitted to the municipal government for approval to collect taxes at the same rate as the southern and northern parts of the city. Now, Wusong rickshaw and small cart pullers, citing that the tax rate is too high and unbearable, have petitioned for a reduction, requesting to operate only within the Wusong district, and are generally unwilling to register. Mr. Shen Risheng, a standing committee member of the Sixth District Party Department, on the one hand, advised the rickshaw companies, and on the other hand, went to the Public Works and Finance Bureaus to represent the cart pullers. The Public Works and Finance Bureaus jointly discussed the matter. As a result, considering the aforementioned situation of the rickshaw and small cart pullers in the district, it was deemed that the tax rate could be appropriately reduced. It was decided that the tax rates for rickshaws and small carts in the district would be temporarily reduced by 50%. In the future, when the central urban area becomes prosperous and there is a considerable need, the full tax will be collected again. However, during the period of reduced tax collection, the business scope of these vehicles will be limited to the Wusong district. The above plan will be implemented after being submitted to the municipal government for approval and then publicly announced.

Language School Preparations Completed 177

The Language Institute at 127 Avenue du Roi Albert, founded by Zhou Xiansheng, Xu Peihuang, Xu Chusheng, and more than ten others, is divided into six departments: Chinese, English, German, French, Russian, and Japanese. The Chinese department is specifically set up for foreigners. Each department is divided into three levels, with a flexible curriculum. Students must complete 120 to 150 credits to graduate. The entrance examination is scheduled for August 15, and classes will begin on September 1. There is a large number of applicants. The close ties of modern international relations have made people in academic and business circles feel the importance of foreign languages. Due to the lack of talent and funding, a school specializing in training in various languages to facilitate international cultural exchange, although long desired by the Chinese people, has not yet been established. Therefore, the establishment of this school is truly the beginning of Chinese language schools.

Two Apprentices Bewitched by Novels 178

Leaving a Message Saying They Are Going to a Deep Mountain to Cultivate Taoism

Novels Mislead People to Such an Extent

The Yongtai Xiang Department Store, located at the corner of West Xinqiao Street on Rue de Consulat in the French Concession, is large in scale and has a decent business. It employs more than thirty clerks and apprentices. Among them are two apprentices: Zhang Wenhua from Kunshan, who is twenty years old, and Lin Zhengting from Ningbo, who is eighteen years old. The two apprentices are quite close. Every evening after closing, when they go upstairs to sleep, they each bring a copy of the latest popular martial arts novel, becoming so addicted to reading that they often talk to their colleagues about wanting to learn the art of flying through the air and serving the country after attaining enlightenment. Their colleagues initially did not suspect anything. However, the day before yesterday, the two apprentices suddenly left at the same time and did not return even late at night. The manager sent people out to search for them everywhere but could not find them. They searched through the items left behind by the two apprentices and found a letter stating that they were going to a deep mountain to cultivate Taoism. The store, concluding that the two apprentices were undoubtedly bewitched by martial arts novels, immediately sent letters to their respective guarantors, informing their families to come to Shanghai to find them, and also reported the matter to the local police station, requesting them to investigate the whereabouts of Zhang and Lin.

Worker Holds Grudge and Kills Foreman 179

Surrenders to the Police Station After the Incident

Jin Niangen, also known as Jin Yigen, a 32-year-old local foreman at the Yangshupu Water Plant, was the director of the paint department and lived at 1089 Pingliang Road. He also owned the Jin Yongchang Paint Shop. Shen Dongsheng, a local worker in the factory, had previously asked Jin for leave to go to Wuxi to recuperate. Later, due to financial difficulties, he sent a letter asking Jin to arrange for money from the factory, which was unsuccessful. In anger, he came to Shanghai around 6:00 AM on the 1st of this month, bought a sharp knife, and waited on Taopeng Road. He stabbed Jin three times in the waist and back. Jin, in pain, ran home. A Chinese police officer, No. 3790, patrolling the street, heard the alarm and sent Jin to Tongren Hospital, where he died despite treatment. The body was taken to the Fielun Road morgue by Chinese detective Zhang Jiaxuan from the Yangshupu Police Station. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the Special District Court, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. He took his seat and, according to Jin Jiangshi, the wife of the deceased, her husband Jin Yigen had been working at the water plant for nine years. The defendant had come before and asked her husband to report to the factory, falsely claiming that he had died of illness, so that the foreigners would give him 200 yuan in compensation. Her husband refused, and the defendant committed this heinous act. At the time, her husband was injured and ran home in pain, covered in blood, saying that he had been stabbed by the defendant with a knife. He was taken to the hospital but died despite treatment. She requested an investigation. The defendant surrendered to the Yangshupu Police Station after the incident. When questioned, he confessed that he had asked for leave due to illness and then asked the deceased to withdraw his savings from the factory. He said that his position had been suspended by the foreigners because he had taken too much sick leave, and he refused to help him in any other way. He was so angry that he bought a knife, waited there, and stabbed him, only intending to vent his anger and not to kill him. He surrendered to the police station afterward. Mr. Guo verified the confession and examined the body, confirming that Jin Yigen had been stabbed to death. The murderer, Shen Liansheng, has been prosecuted by the police station and should be sent to the court for review. The body was handed over to the deceased's wife, Jin Jiangshi, for coffin burial.

Kunshan Kidnapper Arrested in Shanghai 180

Xia Xiaomazi, Sixteen Years Old

Pan Mingshou, a detective from the Kunshan County Government, reported to the French police a few days ago that a kidnapper named Xia Xiaomazi had conspired with accomplices in Kunshan to kidnap someone and extort a large sum of money. After the arrest of accomplices such as Zhou Er Mazi, they confessed that their accomplice Xia Xiaomazi had fled to Shanghai and was hiding in Qiaxing Lane on Xujiahui Road. He requested cooperation in the arrest. The police chief approved the request and immediately ordered the detective to cooperate in arresting Xia and bringing him to the police station. Yesterday, he was brought to the Second Court of the Special District, where Judge Luo Renji took his seat in the criminal court. First, Fei Xizhen, the attorney representing the police station, presented the case, followed by the detective who filed the case, requesting permission to transfer him. When questioned, Xia Xiaomazi confessed that he was from Jiangbei and was sixteen years old. He denied being a thief. Judge Luo ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the hearing.

Ren Zhennan's Wife Files for Legal Separation 181

Requesting 120 Yuan Per Month for Living Expenses

The case in which Ren Jiangshi, the wife of lawyer Ren Zhennan, filed a criminal complaint with the District Court Prosecutor's Office against Ren Zhennan for insult and injury has been dismissed. Now, Ren Jiangshi has again hired lawyer Tao Jiachun to file a petition with the Mediation Office of the District Court for legal separation. Her statement roughly states that due to unbearable abuse, she requests that the court order a legal separation to protect her life. Ms. Ren was born after her father had passed away, leaving her without uncles or brothers. She and her mother relied on her mother's income as a worker to raise her. When she was thirteen years old, her mother arranged for her to marry Ren Zhennan through a matchmaker. Later, Ren Zhennan studied in France, became accustomed to European ways, and became arrogant, extravagant, and licentious, looking down on everyone. When he returned to China, Ms. Ren's family proposed the marriage, but he disliked them for being poor and had someone else he liked, intending to break off the engagement. His father did not allow it, so they reluctantly held the wedding ceremony on May 10 at the Yangjingbang Catholic Church. Because Ren Zhennan's wish was not fulfilled, he harbored resentment. When Ms. Ren's mother went to visit, he thought that because she was working as a servant, her clothes were shabby, and she was his mother-in-law, it was a disgrace to his qualifications as a student who had studied abroad and his status as a lawyer who could afford to ride in a car. Therefore, he abused Ms. Ren even more, forcing her to divorce. Although Ms. Ren's family was poor, she had studied at Chongde Girls' School for several years, believed in Catholicism, and knew some etiquette, so she tolerated it without complaint. However, he became more and more extreme, and everything that people would not do, he did. He was violent, tyrannical, and more fierce than a beast. Ms. Ren realized that if she did not seek help, she would die. Therefore, she went back to her mother's house to live temporarily and filed a complaint with the Prosecutor's Office for injury and legal action to warn the wicked and hope for reform. Unexpectedly, the Prosecutor's Office did not handle the injury case. In addition to requesting a review according to law, the marital relationship was already so bad, and the cruel behavior had not been dealt with according to law. Then his ferocity would be even greater. If she went back, the abuse would be even worse. As a weak woman, how could she protect her life? After thinking it over again and again, she had no choice but to file a petition, weeping and begging the court to investigate, pity her weakness, uphold justice, and provide legal assistance, ordering him to pay living expenses every month, so that she could live with her mother and protect her life. Then not only would Ms. Ren and her mother be eternally grateful, but her late father would also be grateful in the afterlife. Yesterday morning, Judge Chen Bingxin specially opened the Eighth Court for hearing. Ren Zhennan did not appear, only the petitioner Ren Jiangshi and lawyer Tao Jiachun appeared in court. Ms. Ren Jiangshi testified that she was 21 years old, from Ningbo, and lived in her mother's house at No. 11 Dafang Lane, Xiaobeimen. She also stated the previous situation and requested that the legal separation be granted. Lawyer Tao then stated that the petitioner and the defendant were formally married. There was a case in the Prosecutor's Office, and the newspapers reported the criminal part in detail. The pain suffered by the petitioner was difficult to speak about. This time, the petitioner came to our law firm to cry and complain about the past. Our lawyer saw that she was very bitter, so he went to find the defendant's attorneys, Jin Yu, Xue Jiaqi, etc. (because Ren had another case in court and hired lawyers Jin and Xue to represent him) to discuss a mediation plan. They said that Ren did not agree to mediation and was willing to go to court. However, the petitioner's mother was working as a servant and her life was very hard. Therefore, the petitioner requested that living expenses be granted and still intended to study, hoping that the defendant would one day change his mind and the couple would reconcile. Now, she intends to request living expenses of 120 yuan per month (including 30 yuan for rent, 30 yuan for food, 20 yuan for pocket money, 20 yuan for buying clothes, and 20 yuan for education). Considering the defendant's status as a student who had studied in France, a lawyer, and the ability to ride in a car, the request for 120 yuan per month was not excessive. The defendant, as a lawyer, should know the law. He should have appeared in court when summoned. He should be punished for resisting the summons. Now, he requested that the court issue another summons for the defendant to appear in court so that mediation could be facilitated. The judge approved the request and waited for the clerk to issue another summons. Then the court adjourned.

The Danger of Unremoved Wires 182

Worker Xu Er Dies Tragically from Electric Shock

There was a Japanese power plant in front of Zhabei Yokohama Road, which has recently been closed. The building has been sold to someone. Yesterday, the buyer sent several workers to demolish the building. The plant was originally equipped with electric lights. Although the wires inside had been removed, the main power line was not removed from the pole. A worker named Xu Er was holding onto this wire when he was electrocuted and fell down, dying instantly. The local security reported the matter to the District Court, which dispatched prosecutor Wu and others to the scene to investigate. They confirmed that the death was caused by electric shock and ordered the family to collect the body for burial.

Young Woman from Minhang Flees to Shanghai 185

Around 11:00 AM yesterday, Guo Buyun, a police officer at post No. 14 in front of the Nanshi Municipal Party Department, found a young woman who appeared to be lost, wearing a small blue and white floral print jacket, blue old cloth pants, black socks, and cloth shoes.
