A Glimpse of the Third Year of the Child Welfare Association 186

Dr. Wu Weide, the director-general of the Child Welfare Association, announced the general situation of the association's work in the third year and stated that the association's policy would undergo major changes in the future. According to him:

Policy Change: At the beginning of the association's establishment, all kinds of affairs started from the relief end. After discussion by the executive committee, it was generally believed that the association's work should cover the whole country. Its nature is universal, not local; national, not regional; educational, not relief. In the future, it is necessary to unite comrades across the country, think from the root, and carry out large-scale publicity, so as to awaken the people across the country and jointly promote progress.

Registration Completed: On May 24 last year, the association was issued Certificate No. 1 of the Ci character by the Shanghai Municipal Party Department's People's Training Committee. On September 25, an order for sound organization and training was issued. Subsequently, it was registered with the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs. On September 30, Certificate No. 3 of the Shan character was issued, and a wooden seal of Shan character No. 48 was issued. The registration procedures can be said to be complete.

Organizing Branches: This spring, the association received letters from enthusiastic child welfare advocates in Nanjing, Beiping, Guangzhou, Hangzhou, Hankou, etc., inquiring about the organization of child welfare branches. According to the association's charter, there are only provisions for branch offices. With the approval of the Bureau of Social Affairs, the word "branch" was added to the charter. The outline of the branch organization was also formulated and submitted to the Executive Committee for approval and implementation.

Child Protection: The association's organization is divided into five departments. The Child Protection Department handled 72 cases of child abuse in this year, of which 62 were investigated on-site and 10 were investigated by correspondence. The methods of handling included taking abused children into the association's care, sending them to relief homes, returning them to their guardians, and filing lawsuits on their behalf, requesting the court to punish the parties involved. All decisions were made according to the circumstances at the time. A plan to release Shanghai's young prostitutes is now being drawn up and will be carried out in cooperation with the Women and Children Relief Association to facilitate progress.

Child Education: The association is affiliated with the Ciyou Education Institute, whose purpose is to enable children without families to have a good relationship with families without children. On the one hand, it tries to adopt them, and on the other hand, it allows people to take them away, so that orphaned children can each have a place to live. In this year, a total of 67 children were adopted and 40 children were sent for adoption. There are still 27 children remaining. On May 16 of this year, the institute held a wedding ceremony for a female student, Sun Fengzhi. Dr. Luo Yunyan, vice president of the association, presided over the wedding, and Hu Yigu, judge of the Jiangsu Higher Court, served as the wedding witness. The Social Security Bureau also sent representatives to supervise the wedding. The ceremony was quite grand.

Child Health: The association has two Ciyou medical clinics in Zhabei and Yangshupu. In this year, a total of 21,082 sick children were cured. In June last year, a health campaign was held in Zhabei. It is estimated that more than 3,000 people participated in the opening ceremony, more than 1,000 people joined the lantern parade, and about 40,000 people visited the exhibition and movies. In June of this year, children's health campaigns were held successively in Zhabei and Yangshupu. It is estimated that more than 5,000 people participated in the opening ceremony, 4,000 people participated in the lantern parade, and about 80,000 people visited the exhibition and movies.

Child Research: In April of this year, the association founded a Ciyou Garden in Yangshupu to study the physiological and psychological needs of children. Most of the children admitted are children of workers, limited to two to four years old. Every morning, when workers go to work, they send their children to the garden. The garden provides lunch and appropriate education. In the afternoon, when workers get off work, they take them back. Currently, Professor Chen Heqin, director of the Chinese Education Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, is the honorary director, Mrs. Haimu Hua is the honorary director, and Mrs. Wang Guanyi is the full-time teacher. The management is quite perfect.

Social Education: The Ciyou Monthly, published by the association, was registered with the Ministry of Internal Affairs in April of this year. It has now been published in Volume 2, Issue 3. It is still edited by Mr. Chen Zhengfan. The content is quite substantial and wonderful. The association also published three types of Ciyou series of books: (1) How to Teach Children (written by Professor Chen Heqin), (2) Sparrow and Family Education (written by Chen Zhengfan), (3) Creating a Good Environment for Children (written by Professor Chen Heqin), which are widely sold. Other publications, such as Children's Education Pictures, Children's Song Collections, and Children's Story Collections, are also very popular in society. The association also promoted the meaning and importance of Children's Day. People from all walks of life responded enthusiastically. The National Government has now officially stipulated that April 4 is China's Children's Day, and the Ministry of Education has formulated commemorative measures, which must be implemented nationwide every year.

When they returned to Shanghai, it was already late at night. The remaining three factories, Yifeng, Zhaofeng, and Yufeng, could not be visited due to the late hour.

Inspection of Ships Arriving from Ningbo 190

Rapid Quarantine for Passenger Convenience

The Municipal Health Bureau and the Harbor Quarantine Office will jointly inspect ships arriving from Ningbo and provide passengers with free vaccinations, effective from August 1. Yesterday morning, at 3:00 AM, the Xin Beijing and Ningshao ships arriving from Ningbo arrived at Sanjia Water outside the Wusongkou. Three quarantine officers boarded each ship to carry out quarantine and provide free vaccinations. Director Hu of the Municipal Health Bureau also went to Wusong at night to give instructions. To take care of the convenience of merchants and travelers, the ships were allowed to proceed as usual after the quarantine officers boarded. The shipowners knew that quarantine was to protect public health and was a common practice in civilized commercial ports, so they led the crew to assist in the process. Passengers also welcomed the free vaccinations. It is estimated that more than 500 people were vaccinated on the Ningshao ship and more than 900 people were vaccinated on the Xin Beijing ship. Half an hour before the ship arrived at the dock, the quarantine and vaccinations on each ship had been completed. The process was very rapid and convenient for the shipping industry and travelers. This was because the Municipal Health Bureau and the Harbor Quarantine Office had made meticulous considerations in advance on both epidemic prevention and convenience for merchants and travelers, so the process went smoothly.

Wusong Chamber of Commerce Complies with Order to Cease Operations 195

The Wusong Chamber of Commerce continued to argue its case after its seal was confiscated. Subsequently, it received a response from the Training Department of the Central Party Headquarters stating that the Wusong Chamber of Commerce was not needed as a separate entity. The committee members of the Chamber seemed to have doubts about the interpretation of the proviso in Article 5 of the Chamber of Commerce Law and immediately telegraphed the Judicial Yuan requesting an interpretation. The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce also sent a telegram on their behalf. The Chamber has now received a respectful telegram from the Judicial Yuan stating that since the Central Training Department has deemed that Wusong does not need a separate Chamber of Commerce, no further explanation is necessary. As such, the Chamber has complied with the order to cease operations and has announced this to the public in the newspapers. However, a concrete solution for the Chamber's assets and past debts has not yet been reached, and creditors have not made any statements. The conclusion to this issue remains unknown.

Tragic Disaster in Tanghe and Other Counties in Henan 199

Report from the Jisheng Society

According to a report from the Henan Province Tanghe County Bandit Disaster Relief Association to the China Jisheng Society, Tanghe County has been plagued by disasters since the 17th year of the Republic [1928]. The city was first captured by the bandit Li, then by the Red Bandits, and then by the bandit Cui. On May 30th, at dawn, Cui's bandits, with approximately 10,000 men and guns and over 1,000 horses, broke into the city and occupied it for 18 days. They disturbed an area over a hundred miles away, and all men, women, old and young were bound. Rich and poor alike were tied up. Demands for money impoverished families, and extortions left them destitute. Any delay resulted in torture and whipping, and those who exceeded the deadline were immediately beheaded. The number of people having their noses, ears, fingers, and feet cut off daily was in the hundreds. Nineteen out of ten houses in the city were burned, and all clothing and belongings were swept clean. Everywhere they dug and scraped, truly stripping the land bare. The population was reduced by more than half, and no family was spared, not even the chickens and dogs. Not a single pot or stove remained in any home. The streets were filled with the heads and tails of pigs and sheep, and the sights were filled with the corpses of the dead. The chaos of Li Zicheng's rebellion was nothing compared to this. In the countryside, nearly a hundred miles from the county seat, there were almost no traces of civilians. The wheat that was about to be harvested was abandoned in the fields. The remaining grain was burned. All the villages were burned, and the population was dragged away. There were no livestock in the fields, and the villages were reduced to scorched earth. The wells and ruins were desolate, and the four suburban areas were barren. Starving people lined the roads, and it was difficult to avoid death. More than 20,000 people were taken away as hostages, and the loss of property exceeded tens of thousands. On July 11th, they were again hit by torrential rains. The Tang, Tong, and Bi rivers simultaneously swelled, flooding areas of more than ten miles east to west and more than a hundred miles north to south. Aside from those who died at the hands of bandits, many also drowned. The survivors do not know how to live out their remaining days. They are appealing for rescue, unable to wait any longer. It is reported that in Henan Province, Xinyang, Guangshan, Luoshan, Gushi, Shangcheng, Yexian, Dengxian, Nantai, Tongbai, Nanyang, Songxian, Yiyang, Menyang, Wuyang, Lushi, Xinye, Xinan, Zhechuan, Yancheng, Qixian, and other counties have suffered from banditry or natural disasters, or both. Dozens of counties have reported, and who knows how many have not yet reported. With such a major catastrophe looming, the displaced people have nowhere to flee. It is impossible to save everyone. The misery is unbearable. It is hoped that our charitable comrades can do their best to save as many lives as possible, as this is the greatest merit. Saving others is saving oneself, and helping others is creating blessings. Let all comrades pay attention to this. The natural disaster is so great, and the man-made disaster is so cruel. Those with a heart who read this report will surely be moved and unable to remain indifferent.

Report on Good Deeds of Tongren Fuyuantang 201

Report on the good deeds of Tongren Fuyuantang in July: (1) Food rations: assistance to 323 widows, 345 disabled individuals, poverty relief to 99 individuals, security assistance to 103 individuals (each of the above four items received one yuan); aid to 50 orphans (each received 80 cents), totaling 910 yuan. (2) Coffin distribution: 87 large coffins and 66 small coffins to Xin Puyu Hall, 18 large coffins to Jiangsu Second Prison, 22 large coffins and 68 small coffins to various hospitals and door-to-door distribution, 67 large coffins and 75 small coffins to Tongren Fuyuantang branch, 29 large coffins and 78 small coffins to Tongren Fuyuantang Rescue Bureau, totaling 510 large and small coffins distributed. (3) Burial: Tongren Fuyuantang buried 105 large coffins and 212 small coffins, the Tongren Fuyuantang branch buried 67 large coffins and 339 small coffins, and the Tongren Fuyuantang Rescue Bureau buried 55 large coffins and 145 small coffins, totaling 933 large and small coffins buried. (4) Medical care: 1,620 traditional Chinese medicine consultations, 734 Western medicine consultations, totaling 2,354 consultations. All necessary Chinese and Western medicines are provided by the hall without additional charges. Furthermore, the management of coffin burials in the area from Qichang Dock in Pudong, east to Yangjingzhen, west to Shibaba Jian, south to Tangqiao, and north to Huangpu, which was previously handled by the Pushan Villa, has been taken over by Tongren Fuyuantang, which has sent personnel to manage it since July 1st. A total of 136 small coffins have been buried. The directors and deputy directors, Qin Yanqi and Zhu Qingsheng, have created a register and submitted it to the Social Bureau for record.

Book and Newspaper Recommendations

A Brief Discussion of Nietzsche's Philosophy of the Superman 215

— Yu Yang

Written by Li Shicen, Published by Commercial Press

Yesterday, I happened to see a newly published book by Mr. Li Shicen at the Commercial Press, "A Brief Discussion of Nietzsche's Philosophy of the Superman," which made me very happy. Books on the study of Nietzsche's thought are almost non-existent in China (except for short introductory articles). Mr. Li Shicen is known for introducing Nietzsche's ideas, and I heard that he recently spent a long time studying in Germany. How appropriate and insightful it is for him to write this book! After buying it and returning home, I happily read it in one breath. Although it is a small booklet of less than a hundred pages (ninety-four pages), I feel that it allows one to glimpse the general ideas of the outstanding and extraordinary philosopher of the Superman, giving our aging nation a shot in the arm. Therefore, I cannot help but introduce it.

Why does the author want to introduce the thought of this philosopher of the Superman? We see these words on the first page of the introduction:

The reason why I am so eager to introduce Nietzsche's thought is complex, but generally speaking, it can be divided into several points:

(1) Nietzsche's meaning in creating the philosophy of the Superman is because all of humanity is too weak, too cheap, too idealistic, and too greedy for ease. I wish to introduce the philosophy of the Superman because China is too weak, too cheap, too idealistic, and too greedy for ease...

(2) The biggest weakness of the Chinese nation is its compromising and lukewarm nature. On the surface, this seems like moderation and peace, but in reality, it is just the exposure of the inferior nature of hypocrites and slaves. This nature has been passed down for a long time, and it is not easy to awaken without a great stimulus and thorough awakening. This is my second reason for introducing Nietzsche's thought.

(3) Nietzsche's philosophy is a philosophy of resistance, a philosophy of anti-values. Nietzsche called for "a re-evaluation of all values." But Nietzsche's target of resistance is the cannibalistic Christianity. This book, however, wants to attack the cannibalistic rites and customs...

(4) The Chinese nation does not outwardly believe in any religion, but in its bones it believes in polytheism... Nietzsche shouts out, "It is permissible to blaspheme, because God is already dead." What a powerful proverb! Without breaking the idea of polytheism, the authority of science cannot be exerted. This is my fourth reason for introducing Nietzsche's thought.

Nietzsche's thought has been cursed a lot after the European War, believing that it can promote war. These are all exaggerated remarks. In China, we should not think like this, but should sincerely welcome this lofty and great thought in order to revive the declining and rise up from the ruins.

The structure of the whole book is divided into the following chapters: (1) Introduction, (2) A Short Biography of Nietzsche, (3) The Development Process of Nietzsche's Thought, (4) Nietzsche and Stirner, (5) Nietzsche and Schopenhauer, (6) Nietzsche's View of Life, (7) Nietzsche's View of the Universe, (8) Nietzsche's View of Values, (9) Nietzsche's View of Evolution, (10) Nietzsche's View of Morality, (11) Nietzsche's View of Art, (12) Conclusion. This is very natural and comprehensive. Please add a brief explanation below:

In "A Short Biography of Nietzsche," the life of this philosopher of the Superman is narrated purely from the perspective of simple thought, and it concludes that "Nietzsche's egoism did not come from suffering, loneliness, and depression, but from the essence of his personality. From the essence of his personality came his 'truth' and 'greatness'." The author is truly a confidant of Nietzsche. In "The Development Process of Nietzsche's Thought," the evolutionary principle believed by Nietzsche—that by the age of thirty, one must replay the evolutionary process of mankind from the first ancestor to modern man over three thousand years—is used to explain the development of Nietzsche's own thought, and Nietzsche's works are used as evidence. The first period is represented by "The Birth of Tragedy" and "Untimely Meditations," the second period is represented by "Human, All Too Human" and "Dawn," and the third period is represented by "The Gay Science," Thus Spoke Zarathustra, "Beyond Good and Evil," "On the Genealogy of Morality," "The Case of Wagner," "Twilight of the Idols," "Nietzsche contra Wagner," "The Antichrist," and "Ecce Homo." This is a systematic arrangement. Then, these works are further explained, and it is concluded that "the first period is the Romantic period, the second period is the Naturalistic period, and the third period is the Neo-Romantic period." The third period is considered the most important, but the first and second periods should not be ignored. This chapter clearly explains the complicated developmental process of the Superman philosopher’s thought effortlessly, which is a pleasant thing for the reader.

The two chapters "Nietzsche and Stirner" and "Nietzsche and Schopenhauer" explain that Schopenhauer was the starting point for guiding Nietzsche's philosophy, and Stirner guided the entirety of Nietzsche's philosophy. Stirner discovered that "the only thing that truly exists in the universe is my self." Nietzsche then accepted Stirner's proposition and achieved his philosophy of the Superman. Nietzsche inherited Schopenhauer's will theory and further expanded it, transforming Schopenhauer's will to live into the will to power. These two chapters explain the relationship between Nietzsche and the thoughts of these two men, conducting a tracing of the roots and origins of Nietzsche's theory.

From the sixth to the eleventh chapters, these are the central points of the book. The narration of "Nietzsche's View of Life" uses the book "The Birth of Tragedy" as its basis, recognizing this book as the crystallization of (1) classical philology, (2) Schopenhauer's philosophy of will, and (3) the influence of Wagner's music. From classical philology, one obtains the two spiritual trends of Greece—with the god of beauty and the god of wine representing these two spirits, evolving into the world of static beauty and the world of will—Schopenhauer's philosophy of will inspires the thought of the will to power, and Wagner's music promotes artistic taste. From these three influences, Nietzsche's view of life is achieved—the first essential of life is to take a challenging attitude towards life, and to exchange the greatest pain for a noble life. The end of this chapter further uses Nietzsche's view of life to criticize the Chinese view of life. Speaking of "Nietzsche's View of the Universe," it first narrates Nietzsche's use of sharp and courageous eyes to break all "realistic thoughts" (the essence of the universe) that originate from illusion worship, and then builds his own "eternal recurrence theory," saying that the truth of the universe is inevitable, decided, fatalistic, and blind. Nietzsche's focus is on making the universe extremely stale and meaningless, and then the Superman will pull it back with one hand, reviving the stale and enriching the meaningless, so the Superman is valuable in fighting against the god of death, fighting against fate, and making a struggle against eternal recurrence.

In "Nietzsche's View of Values," the Superman philosophy published in his masterpiece "Thus Spoke Zarathustra" is explained. He only values the earth and not heaven, only values the flesh and not the spirit, re-evaluating the standard of value, believing that whatever makes "life" more beautiful is good, otherwise it is evil; whatever makes "life" stronger is good, otherwise it is evil; whatever makes "life" full and expanded is good, otherwise it is evil. Using such thoughts to criticize the Chinese people's values is indeed completely useless. "Nietzsche's View of Evolution" explains that his observations are similar to Darwin's—that mankind can evolve into the Superman, but there are two major boundaries. Darwin believes that life is a struggle for survival, while Nietzsche believes that life has a competition beyond survival. Darwin emphasizes external forces, taking the environment as the reason for evolution, while Nietzsche emphasizes internal forces, taking the will to power as the reason for evolution. This is a very powerful explanation.

In the chapter "Nietzsche's View of Morality," based on his book "Beyond Good and Evil," morality is divided into two categories: (1) the morality of great men, and (2) the morality of slaves. The so-called morality of great men is the morality of actively affirming the self, satisfying instincts, and possessing the highest value. On the contrary, the morality of slaves is the morality of merely using the power of the majority, the revelation of God, the authority of the state, and the legends of society to oppress the strong and great, making mankind fall into decay and corruption day by day, which is a morality of absolutely no value. The morality of great men is the "morality of war," and the so-called war is for mankind, for life, and for the Superman. This is the standard of the morality of war. Nietzsche further divides the process of war into three types: (1) from spirit to camel, (2) from camel to lion, and (3) from lion to child. Therefore, the morality of war also possesses these three spirits. Finally, "Nietzsche's View of Art" explains that Nietzsche particularly values the art of living, as well as the essence of art that he discovered, and the indispensable elements of artists. These two chapters both use Nietzsche's thought to criticize the Chinese people's moral concepts and artistic concepts.

The conclusion of the whole book makes a simple comparison of the three famous individualists of the nineteenth century, Nietzsche, Stirner, and Kierkegaard, in order to elucidate the true meaning of individualism. The author even loudly proclaims:

"When Chinese people hear the term 'individualism,' they will immediately associate it with selfishness, thinking that it is an ominous thing. Little do they know that the main purpose of individualism is to actively affirm the self, affirm the self's personality, and affirm the self's life. Self-affirmation makes the whole world affirm, and one will realize that one should have a responsibility to the world, and one should also have a responsibility to oneself."

The above has introduced a general outline of the book "A Brief Discussion of Nietzsche's Philosophy of the Superman." When reading this book, one can only feel that the introduction is extremely systematic, the explanation is extremely thorough, and the sharpness of the writing and the richness of the vocabulary are like the author's attitude when he is lecturing on the podium, making people forget their weariness. In the important chapters of this book, the author always concludes by using Nietzsche's thought to criticize the traditional concepts of the Chinese people. When reading, one can only feel that it hits the nail on the head and is extremely enjoyable. The Chinese nation has entered a state of aging and decline today. The transformation of human nature is even more important than all transformations. To transform human nature, one cannot but inject this forceful shot in the arm from Nietzsche. The author, borrowing Nietzsche's tone, said:

"If you do not believe that the truth that Nietzsche preaches is true, then you youths who are not awakened have no reason to exist!"

Are the readers moved? Please take the time to savor this book.

Social News

A New Application of the Periscope 217

— Jun Shan

The periscope used in submarines to view the sea surface, and by soldiers in trenches to view outside the trench, is now very popular in the United States. It is just that the application has changed from military to entertainment. An inventor who is good at speculation has made many miniature periscopes, beautifully decorated, and specializes in selling them to a group of people who love to watch sports games. With one of these in hand, you don't have to squeeze to the front to see the details of the game. Just leisurely wait behind people, hold up the periscope to look, and naturally you won't miss any of the excitement of the game. This is good news for short spectators!

At the Hospital 218

— Hai Fan

On Saturday (June 27th) at 9:10 am, because of my friend Kai Jun's illness, I stepped into the door of a hospital by the Wusong seaside. The first impression we got was a registration clerk who looked neither like a winter melon nor a short pumpkin. It was time to register, but he was busy with his own work. After several questions, he began to do what he should have done.

The unlucky person (patient) is really haunted by ghosts. Coincidentally, the Dean Yi Ye (I know this from their title), with a Rock cigarette holder in his mouth, swaggered in. When he got to the door, he said, "You (pointing to the registration clerk) make a phone call for me to the arsenal to ask Mr. Wang (forgive me for not hearing clearly) whether the business he introduced to me is going to happen." In this way, the Dean's phone call was naturally a victory, and the patient's registration was naturally a failure. The phone call back said that the business was available, and there was even a house call, but the time could be arranged. Who knew that our hospital's Dean, upon hearing the words "house call," without asking about the time, immediately put on a smiling face and went to the Dean's office to change clothes.

This Dean's office is opposite the registration desk. On the wall hangs a sign with the three characters (Dean's Office). In addition, it is a transparent glass window, so you can see it so clearly. By the time the Dean had changed his clothes, there were more than twenty patients registering for surgery, but they were all workers. There was only my friend Kai Jun registering for internal medicine. As a result, when the Dean went on a house call, he took five minutes (at most) to diagnose my friend Kai Jun alone, which made me unable to help but be grateful. However, in the diagnosis, he hastily wrote two vague words that I couldn't tell whether they were English or German, and then added a question mark at the end, which made me unable to avoid suspicion, because I was anxious to know what illness my friend had, I could not help but ask:

"Dean, what exactly is his illness?"

Not only did he not answer, but he didn't even look at me, and went on the house call with his female nurse, sitting in two rickshaws.

The next day, Kai Jun's illness worsened. For the sake of my friend's illness, I had no choice but to swallow my anger and still ran to the hospital where I had been snubbed to inquire about the rules for hospitalization. Just in time, I met the very imposing Dean from yesterday, forcing me to call out:

"Dean, does your hospital have any quieter rooms?" (referring to the four-person rooms).

But he replied with a sarcastic and angry tone, "We can't build another house just for your friend here."

I thought he was really strange. He hadn't even answered whether there were any rooms yet, and he treated people with this kind of attitude. I was just about to retort, but he left. For the sake of my friend's illness, I had no choice but to return to school.

Here comes another snag. No. 8 Li Family Residence is home to someone surnamed Wang. He is my friend, one could say my best friend. He has a special temper and doesn't like to socialize with people. Sometimes, he is even too lazy to talk to people. At the same time, he also has a different kind of malaria. When this disease doesn't break out, it doesn't break out, but when it does, he faints. Not only can he not speak, but he can only move his hands and feet slightly. The appearance of his eyes is dull, looking like someone who is about to die, except that his breathing is different.

On the 23rd, because of an inadvertent mistake, he brought on his old illness that had not broken out for several years. The situation was no different from what I described earlier, so the people living with him were terrified. They wanted to send him to the hospital, but they were afraid that if something unfortunate happened, no one would be responsible. If they didn't send him to the hospital, they would be guilty of conscience for not saving someone who was about to die. It was really difficult to decide. After hesitating for a while, they finally came to call me. When I saw that kind of situation, I only advocated sending him to the hospital. However, besides that hospital, there was no other epidemic hospital to be found. As the saying goes, "When people reach the edge of a cliff, who dares not to bow their heads?" This is my actual situation. When I arrived at that hospital, it just so happened that they were eating. It was truly bad timing and an unfortunate fate. Although the registration was a special registration, the result was exactly the opposite. People with acute illnesses certainly don't feel it, but people with clear minds standing in the open air waiting for half an hour is really unbearable. I don't think eating a home-cooked meal is necessarily more urgent than diagnosing an acute illness.

Alas!

Social News Submission Guidelines 219

(1) The text should be related to domestic and foreign science, industry, commerce, and rural areas.

(2) News about hygiene, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life is limited. Books should be limited to lyrical works about social life.

(3) Photographs are qualified if they are about seasons, scenery, animals and plants, people, and news photography. Photographs of ladies in seasonal scenery are especially welcome.
